msg:We actually booked two rooms for 2&3 nights each. This is based on one of the rooms. 

Location- depends what‚Äôs on your schedule. If Disney is a must then I think it‚Äôs perfect. Lots a families here with kids seemed to be going to Disney. But if you‚Äôd also like to do shopping and walk around the city, it‚Äôs pretty far even with the subway station nearby. The Kerry Parkside doesn‚Äôt have many shops. And we made a mistake as we need to travel back and forth between the hotel and Hong Qiao Station and even the taxi ride was more then an hour each way. 

Service: the check in wasn‚Äôt that pleasant. I came in with a toddler on my arms and a luggage but no one offered help with the luggage. The staff did checked me in earlier around 12:40 which is helpful. But then when I asked another staff which way was the rooms she answered me ‚Äúgo straight‚Äù without even lifting her head up ( I suppose she was busy with something else on her desk?!) not a big deal but quite surprising cold though. 
The service centre staff on the call were all super responsive and accommodating. I asked for a change of bed sheets and amenities for my child and they sent up staff immediately. The cleaning ladies were also very friendly and my toddler even wanted to play with them. 

Room - to my surprise the room was quite old and very damp. Even the sheets felt damp too. We called the service centre and asked for a change of sheets and a dehumidifier. They sent up everything immediately. The water tank of the dehumidifier was full every 3~4 hours. 
We didn‚Äôt book executive rooms so there was no coffee machine in the room just to be aware of. But the mini bar was free so you can get a little snack and drinks. 
There isn‚Äôt anything for kids in the regular rooms even when we booked with a kid on the guest list. But you can call and ask. They brought up kids amenities up as per requested. 
  
Overall, I think most of the staff here are friendly and helpful. Location is average. Regular rooms ( can‚Äôt judge the executive rooms as we didn‚Äôt stay in one of those) definitely need to be upgraded especially the humidity situation. And coffee machine should be provided in all rooms.

Breakfast is free for children under 6 years old, and older children are also OK. Parent-child It should be considered a good hotel, thumbs up!
2. Free minibar + swimming fitness in the first round. It will be replenished on Mondays and Thursdays. There will be beer, juice, biscuits, etc., but no fruit. The swimming pool is 20 meters long and there are two paddling pools. Children should like it very much. The water temperature is OK. There are many children learning to swim. I went for a swim in the afternoon. , I feel that the water quality is average; you have to bring your own bath towels and slippers, the passage to the locker room and swimming pool is very cold; the gym is large, which is relatively good.
3. The food is acceptable. You can go for group buying at the self-service on the first floor, which costs less than 300 for adults, and half price for children over 6 years old. The boss is very generous, and children just over 6 years old are free of charge! So that‚Äôs also a plus. To be honest, the food is quite average, definitely not a five-star restaurant, but at this price, it's still okay. The crab is really cute, the steak must be cooked well, and the red wine is really good.
4. The children's center slide is indeed very interesting. Children like it very much. One free place is provided for each room. It costs 200 per person at one's own expense, valid for two days. Friends with large tonnage should be careful to slow down when taking children to play on the slide, as the inertia is large. In terms of time, it is usually at night. By 7 o'clock, it is probably open separately, which is different from other family hotels.
5. There is a Disney shuttle bus. We chose to leave at 10:30, mainly because there are many people on Valentine's Day, and there will be queues if we go early. In addition, the children can't get up, so we will return at 10 p.m. I didn‚Äôt buy an early access card and played a total of 9 projects. I must rent a stroller! Try not to bring your own. If it doesn‚Äôt meet the park‚Äôs requirements, the money you deposit will be enough to rent a car!
6. The geographical location is superior and the surrounding environment is very good! I looked at more than 10 five-star hotels before and finally chose this one. Considering that it is very convenient to go to Disney's Bund, there are subways and shopping malls downstairs of the hotel. The nearby Century Park has a beautiful environment and must be visited.
7. Finally, I want to talk about the service, which is also commendable. I gave him 2 band-aids in a row. Thank you very much! It's a pity that I didn't remember the handsome guy's name; I asked for a few bottles of water in advance when I went out, and they were delivered quickly, and the service response was timely; the front desk, concierge, and car were very attentive. If you have to be picky, there should be room for improvement compared to other five-star hotels in terms of bringing guests to the room, smiling service, etc.
In short, it was a good Spring Festival trip to Shanghai. It was an unforgettable and wonderful trip. The whole family was very satisfied. Thank you very much to Ctrip and the hotel!

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Stayed in June 2022
info:Family
info:5 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted July 5, 2022
msg:After a year, I chose a parent-child hotel in Shanghai - Kerry Hotel Pudong, and experienced a staycation.
In fact, I have been fond of Kerry Hotel Pudong for a long time, just taking advantage of the inconvenience of leaving Shanghai during this time, I chose a two-day and one-night hotel tour. Our check-in is on the 3rd floor of the hotel, the executive hall, which is also the floor where we have breakfast the next day. Although it is said that we can only check in at 2 o'clock, we arrived at 12:30 and can also check in. We booked a double room. The bed is big, two big and one small are definitely no problem. The bathroom has a shower and a bathtub, and it is also dry and wet. But looking out of the window, it is the International Exhibition Center. If you recommend it, you can pay attention here. We simply packed our luggage and headed straight to this destination, the Internet Celebrity Children's Adventure Park. Since the hotel swimming pool was not open to the public when we went there at the end of June, to go to the children's adventure park, we need to take the elevator to the first floor, then go through the lobby and take another elevator to the fourth floor.
The children's playground is divided into two areas. The outside is suitable for children under 6 years old to play, and the inside is suitable for children and adults to play at the same time. The most distinctive feature of this Internet celebrity children's adventure park is their three major slides. There are long slides that sit on straw mats and are suitable for all children of all ages. This is the only slide where older friends can take children with them. The second one is the blue slide, which is suitable for children over 4 years old. I personally think the height is three stories high. The blue slide has a smooth transition in the middle with an ocean ball at the bottom. The third is the craziest red slide, suitable for children over 7 years old, and the red slide is divided into two different heights. I personally think that one is six-storey high and the other is seven-storey high, and there is no transition in between, people are almost fell vertically. Long-sleeved trousers must be worn on the blue and red slides to prevent scratches. As a friendly reminder, all children and adults who go to the playground to play in the playground should not bring water bottles into the arena. This time, during the play process, a water bottle full of water fell from the top of the slide. Fortunately, no one was hit this time. If it was hit, the injury would be serious. If you need to drink water, there is a place for parents to rest next to the children's playground for children under 6 years old. You can drink water and eat some snacks.
We only tried the straw slide this time, and after playing for two days in a row, the children realized the fun of playing alone. As for me personally, the first time I played the straw slide, it was also very loud. As for the other two slides, we didn't try either this time. Park tickets are valid for 24 hours, which means you can play for two consecutive days. The hotel package we booked this time also includes K20 parent-child activities, and the location of the activities is also in the children's paradise. The content of our activity this time is to paste beans, that is, children choose a pattern, then paste beans of different colors, and finally need to iron. The finished product can be used as coaster. The whole process can exercise children's concentration and patience. It takes about an hour or so.
The package also includes breakfast on the second day. Although there are not many varieties, the environment is good with few people, and the service is also very nice. You can also apply for late check-out. Compared with outdoor activities in hot summer, this kind of indoor air conditioner can also allow children to play independently, freeing parents' hands, and the whole trip is relatively easy. If there is a chance, we will brush again.

i've just stayed Kerry hotel with my family for new years holiday.
my family: 2adult and 3child(ages 10,8,6)
the second day was my daughter's birthday so staff of Kerry hotel prepared a birthday cake and birthday presents as surprise.present are not only for the child who is birthday today but also for another children.
our children was very happy due to  the surprise.cake tasted good very delicious.we are going to display the present for spring holiday next month.
swimming pools are good.
adventure land also good for children.
breakfast is delicious.
so i highly recommend against family who has child under around 13 years old.
i want to stay again if i have other opportunity.
at this time we made some very beautiful memories.
Thank you Kerry hotel.
